		Translate(Config_Options, true, "CreateNewIssuer",
				"Bloomberg_DL_Syndicated_Loans"), "NO_SILENT"))
	return "REFERENCE";

		"Bloomberg_DL_Syndicated_Loans")))

		Translate(Config_Options, true, "CreateNewIssuer",
				"Bloomberg_DL_Syndicated_Loans"), "YES", "NO", "NO_SILENT"))
	return ThrowMapError(
			Strcat(Translate(Config_Options, true, "CreateNewIssuer",
					"Bloomberg_DL_Syndicated_Loans"),
					Strcat("--",
							"Wrong value in Config_Option.xml against CreateNewIssuer  - Bloomberg_DL_Syndicated_Loans. It is other than permitted value YES, NO, NO_SILENT and 'null' used in Config_option.xml")),
			"");

	return "";]]></expr>

			return Translate(BloombergETT, true, "BB_CURRENCY", CRNCY);
		else
			return CRNCY;
	else if (Strcmp(Translate(Config_Options, true, "Convert_To_ISO_Currency", "Bloomberg_DL_Syndicated_Loans"), "ISO"))
		if (OneHasValue(Translate(BloombergETT, true, "BB_CURRENCY", CRNCY)))
			return Translate(BloombergETT, true, "BB_CURRENCY", CRNCY);

			return CRNCY;

		if (OneHasValue(Translate(BloombergETT, true, "BLOOMBERG_CURRENCY_CODE", CRNCY)))
			return Translate(BloombergETT, true, "BLOOMBERG_CURRENCY_CODE", CRNCY);
		else
			return CRNCY;
	else if (!OneOf(Translate(Config_Options, true, "Convert_To_ISO_Currency", "Bloomberg_DL_Syndicated_Loans"), "NO", "ISO", "ISO_MAJOR"))
		return ThrowMapError(Strcat(Translate(Config_Options, true, "Convert_To_ISO_Currency", "Bloomberg_DL_Syndicated_Loans"), Strcat("--", "Wrong value in Config_Option against Bloomberg_DL_Syndicated_Loans for Convert_To_ISO_Currency_Bloomberg_DL_Syndicated_Loans .
